# Cosmic Horror Index — Textual Evidence Document

Every axis score is grounded in specific passages from canonical texts.
This document provides the full citation chain for audit and review.

---


## Absurdism


### Awe Madness
**Score: 62.8** (CI: [42.1, 78.4], n=14 passages)

### Cyclical Destruction
**Score: 78.1** (CI: [63.7, 86.0], n=15 passages)

#### [absurdism_cyclical_destruction_0]
- **Source:** Dialogues Concerning Natural Religion
- **Reference:** 0.164
- **Translation:** David Hume (1779, public domain, PG#4583)
- **Relevance:** 1.00 | **Valence:** +1.00 | **Confidence:** 0.95
- **Justification:** The passage explicitly describes a cosmological system where 'this world, therefore, with all its events, even the most minute, has before been produced and destroyed, and will again be produced and destroyed, without any bounds and limitations,' which directly articulates cyclical destruction and recreation.

> This is commonly, and I believe justly, esteemed the most absurd system that has yet been proposed; yet I know not whether, with a few alterations, it might not be brought to bear a faint appearance of probability. ### Incomprehensibility
**Score: 71.1** (CI: [47.4, 87.0], n=16 passages)

#### [gnosticism_incomprehensibility_0]
- **Source:** Apocryphon of John
- **Reference:** 47
- **Translation:** Stevan Davies
- **Relevance:** 1.00 | **Valence:** +1.00 | **Confidence:** 1.00
- **Justification:** This passage explicitly states that the One cannot be seen, envisioned, conceived, comprehended, or described in words, directly asserting the complete incomprehensibility of ultimate reality to human faculties.

> The One cannot be seen For no one can envision it The One is eternal For it exists forever The One is inconceivable For no one can comprehend it The One is indescribable For no one can put any words to it.
